# AI ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ç ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó ‡≤π‡≤°‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Å, ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ö‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á? 1960‡≤∞ ‡≤¶‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∂‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤ï‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤à‡≤ó ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤à‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤≤‡≥á ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

‡≤à ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤†‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø, ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å HTML, CSS, ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡´ç‡™ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø AI ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å. ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤à‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤≤‡≥á ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≥å‡≤ï‡∞∞‡±ç‡∞Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤¶ AI ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø, ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å.

AI ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø, ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤≤ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥Å, ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥á‡≤∞, ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø.

‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤®‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. HTML ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤´‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, CSS ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç API ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ç AI ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥Ä‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á.

‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤§‡≤É ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤® ‡≤é‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥á ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø.

‡≤à ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤†‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü, AI ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤á‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å API ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å. ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ChatGPT ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å Claude ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤à‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤® AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø.

## ‚ö° ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤® 5 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

**‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Ü‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó**

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[‚ö° 5 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å] --> B[GitHub ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø]
    B --> C[AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø]
    C --> D[Python ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø]
    D --> E[AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø]
```
- **‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤ 1 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑**: [GitHub Models Playground](https://github.com/marketplace/models/azure-openai/gpt-4o-mini/playground) ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤π‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- **‡≤é‡≤∞‡≤°‡≤®‡≥á 2‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≥ï  ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑**: ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤´‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø AI ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- **‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥Å 3‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≥ï  ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑**: "Code" ‡≤ü_TAB_ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Å 4‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≥ï  ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ö‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: `GITHUB_TOKEN=your_token python test.py`
- **‡≤ê‡≤¶‡≥Å 5‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≥ï  ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤ AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø

**‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç**:
```python
import os
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference",
    api_key="your_token_here"
)

response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "Hello AI!"}],
    model="openai/gpt-4o-mini"
)

print(response.choices[0].message.content)
```

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤π‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü**: 5 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï AI ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø. ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤ï‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¨‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤° ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥Ä‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å:

## üó∫Ô∏è AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤£

```mermaid
journey
    title ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ AI ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤¶‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü
    section AI ‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
      ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï AI ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø: 4: You
      GitHub ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 6: You
      AI ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤§‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 8: You
    section ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£
      Python API ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 5: You
      AI ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü: 7: You
      ‡≤Ö‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ä‡≤®‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 8: You
    section ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø
      ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤™‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 6: You
      ‡≤®‡≥à‡≤ú‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤≤ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 8: You
      ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤• ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 9: You
    section ‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤™‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≥ï‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç
      ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ AI ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 7: You
      ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 8: You
      ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ-‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: 9: You
```
**‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤£ ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ø**: ‡≤à ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤†‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü, ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ChatGPT, Claude ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å Google Bard ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ï AI ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤∂, ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ AI ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø.

## AI ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å: ‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü

‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥Å, ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥ã‡≤£. ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å API‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ü, ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤§‡≤É ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏ ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø, ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø.

AI API ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤Ü‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ-‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø, ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶ ‡≤Ö‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤¶‡≥ã‡≤∑‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≤†‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤Ø ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ó‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤≠‡≥á‡≤¶‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø.

### "‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ AI" ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤®‡≥Å?

‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∂‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤à‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥à‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø. AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤π ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≤∏ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‚Äì ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

**‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤π‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤®‡≥Ü:**
- **‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤® ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤™‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‚Äì ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ñ‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤°‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- **‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤• ‚Äì ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü
- **‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ AI**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤° ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤¨‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥á‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤• ‚Äì ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤∂‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤∞ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü, ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü] --> B[AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø]
    B --> C[‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü]
    C --> D[‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø]
    D --> E[‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü]
    
    F[‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤£ ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ<br/>‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ñ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç] --> B
```
### AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü (‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤Ü‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø)

AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ñ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤™‡≤†‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤° ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤à ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü:
- ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü
- ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡∞Ç‡∞ó‡∞æ ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü
- ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤Ö‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤¶ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≥Ä‡≤® ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤∂‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å_decode_‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥á**: ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£, ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤∂ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü; ‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤Ü ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤™‡≤†‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü.

### GitHub Models ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü?

‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å GitHub Models ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‚Äì ‡≤®‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≥Ü AI ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Æ ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤¶ AI ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∂ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü (‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü, ‡≤à‡≤ó‡≤≤‡≥á ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤õ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤!). ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤°‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® API ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø.

‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤§‡≤É "AI-‡≤Ü‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç", ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó? ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤Ü‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó ‡≤∂‡≥Ç‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ñ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤¶ ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç UI] --> B[‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç API]
    B --> C[GitHub ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø API]
    C --> D[AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü]
    D --> C
    C --> B
    B --> A
```
‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å GitHub Models ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤™‡≤∞-‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤¶ AI ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥á‡≤π‡≤ø ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤´‡≥á‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. [GitHub Models Playground](https://github.com/marketplace/models/azure-openai/gpt-4o-mini/playground) ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£.

## üß† AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞

**‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ**: AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥å‡≤∂‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å AI ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤ú ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤¨‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

![GitHub Models AI Playground ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤´‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å](../../../translated_images/playground.d2b927122224ff8f.kn.png)

**‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å:**
- GPT-4o-mini, Claude ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø (‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≥Ç ‡≤â‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§!)
- ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤Ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤£ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤π ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤î‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ ‡≤¨‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø

‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü "Code" ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø.

![‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü](../../../translated_images/playground-choice.1d23ba7d407f4758.kn.png)

## ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

‡≤π‡≥Ä‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó AI ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤£. ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£ AI ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ. ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å GitHub Models ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤É ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ-‡≤§‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤´‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤µ‡≥Å.

### ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤æ‡≤ó, ‡≤π‡≥Ä‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤≠‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≤°‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤°‡≤ø ‚Äì ‡≤π‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤π‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ã‡≤£:

```python
"""Run this model in Python

> pip install openai
"""
import os
from openai import OpenAI

# ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≥ï‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ GitHub ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç (PAT) ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.
# ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ PAT ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø: https://docs.github.com/en/authentication/keeping-your-account-and-data-secure/managing-your-personal-access-tokens
client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference",
    api_key=os.environ["GITHUB_TOKEN"],
)

response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "",
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "What is the capital of France?",
        }
    ],
    model="openai/gpt-4o-mini",
    temperature=1,
    max_tokens=4096,
    top_p=1
)

print(response.choices[0].message.content)
```

**‡≤à ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü:**
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å: ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞ ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ì‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥Å `'os'`, AI ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≥Å `'OpenAI'`
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** OpenAI ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç GitHub ‡≤® AI ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø OpenAI ‡≤®‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑ GitHub ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø (‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï!)
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** ‡≤¨‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤® "‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç" ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø our ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‚Äì ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≤ï‡≤¶ ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** AI ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤≤ ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü
- **‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü** ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤ ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤†‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å

### ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å: AI ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤∞‡≥Ç‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤ñ‡≥Ü

AI ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® "‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç" ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü:

```python
messages=[
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": "You are a helpful assistant who explains things simply."
    },
    {
        "role": "user", 
        "content": "What is machine learning?"
    }
]
```

**‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≤ï ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø:**
- **‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç**: ‡≤®‡≤ü‡≤® ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‚Äì AI ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å, ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- **‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂
- **‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≥ç**: AI ‡≤® ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞ (‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤, ‡≤Ü‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤á‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü)

**‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ ‡≤ú‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü**: ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤® ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤£:
- **‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂**: ‚Äú‡≤á‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤æ, ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å‚Äù
- **‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂**: ‚Äú‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥á?‚Äù
- **‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü**: ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥á‡≤π‡≤™‡≤∞ ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥á ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤∂‡≥Ü‡≤´‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤

### AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•: ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü

AI API ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ñ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤® ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å:

#### ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® (0.0 ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ 2.0): ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤°‡≥à‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å**: AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡¥™‡µç‡¥∞‡¥µ‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≤® ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø:**
- **Temperature = 0.1**: ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å (‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§)
- **Temperature = 0.7**: ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å (‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤®‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶ ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤§‡≥Ü)
- **Temperature = 1.5**: ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤¨‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡∞æ‡∞§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥ç, ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶ ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü (‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Ö‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤µ)

```python
# ‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤æ ‡≤ä‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ)
response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "What is 2+2?"}],
    temperature=0.1  # ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤É ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤≤‡≥Ç "4" ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
)

# ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤í‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤¶‡≥Å)
response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "Write a creative story opening"}],
    temperature=1.2  # ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø, ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤ï‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
)
```

#### ‡≤ó‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç (1 ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ 4096+): ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å**: AI ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø ‡≤é‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å** (1 ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥Å 0.75 ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø):
- **max_tokens=50**: ‡≤ö‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤ß‡≥Å‡≤∞ (‡≤ü‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü)
- **max_tokens=500**: ‡≤í‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤é‡≤∞‡≤°‡≥Å
- **max_tokens=2000**: ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü

```python
# ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤§, ‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "Explain JavaScript"}],
    max_tokens=100  # ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
)

# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶, ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
response = client.chat.completions.create(
    messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "Explain JavaScript"}],
    max_tokens=1500  # ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∂ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
)
```

#### top_p (0.0 ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ 1.0): ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å**: AI ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤á‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**AI ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤° ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø, ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥å‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü**:
- **top_p=0.1**: ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö 10% ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü (‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§)
- **top_p=0.9**: 90% ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤á‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü (‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤)
- **top_p=1.0**: ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤ ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü (‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø)

**‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü**: ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü "‡≤Ü‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∂ ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø..."
- **‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü top_p**: ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤É "‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø" ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- **‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å top_p**: ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø "‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø", "‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤ò", "‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞", "‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü", "‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞" ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

### ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ç ‡≤í‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≥Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

```python
# ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï, ‡≤∏‡≤§‡≤§ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø (‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤π ‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ñ‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≥ä‡≤ü‡≥ç)
factual_params = {
    "temperature": 0.2,
    "max_tokens": 300,
    "top_p": 0.3
}

# ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø
creative_params = {
    "temperature": 1.1,
    "max_tokens": 1000,
    "top_p": 0.9
}

# ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï, ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø (‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤®)
conversational_params = {
    "temperature": 0.7,
    "max_tokens": 500,
    "top_p": 0.8
}
```

**‡≤à ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≤π‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å**: ‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤µ‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï. ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å (‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü), ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Ç ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø(‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤π‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å). ‡≤à ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.
```

**Here's what's happening in this code:**
- **We import** the tools we need: `os` for reading environment variables and `OpenAI` for talking to the AI
- **We set up** the OpenAI client to point to GitHub's AI servers instead of OpenAI directly
- **We authenticate** using a special GitHub token (more on that in a minute!)
- **We structure** our conversation with different "roles" ‚Äì think of it like setting the scene for a play
- **We send** our request to the AI with some fine-tuning parameters
- **We extract** the actual response text from all the data that comes back

> üîê **Security Note**: Never hardcode API keys in your source code! Always use environment variables to store sensitive credentials like your `GITHUB_TOKEN`.

### Creating a Reusable AI Function

Let's refactor this code into a clean, reusable function that we can easily integrate into our web application:

```python
import asyncio
from openai import AsyncOpenAI

# Use AsyncOpenAI for better performance
client = AsyncOpenAI(
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference",
    api_key=os.environ["GITHUB_TOKEN"],
)

async def call_llm_async(prompt: str, system_message: str = "You are a helpful assistant."):
    """
    Sends a prompt to the AI model asynchronously and returns the response.
    
    Args:
        prompt: The user's question or message
        system_message: Instructions that define the AI's behavior and personality
    
    Returns:
        str: The AI's response to the prompt
    """
    try:
        response = await client.chat.completions.create(
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "system",
                    "content": system_message,
                },
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": prompt,
                }
            ],
            model="openai/gpt-4o-mini",
            temperature=1,
            max_tokens=4096,
            top_p=1
        )
        return response.choices[0].message.content
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"AI API error: {str(e)}")
        return "I'm sorry, I'm having trouble processing your request right now."

# Backward compatibility function for synchronous calls
def call_llm(prompt: str, system_message: str = "You are a helpful assistant."):
    """Synchronous wrapper for async AI calls."""
    return asyncio.run(call_llm_async(prompt, system_message))
```

**‡≤à ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤´‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å:**
- ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ê‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤õ‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤é‡≤∞‡≤°‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ñ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤™‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤´‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≤¶ ‡≤°‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç API ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü
- ‡≤∏‡≤§‡≤§ AI ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü

### ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤≤: AI ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç

‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å AI ‡≤Ø ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó, ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å AI ‡≤Ø ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤ê‡≤é‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥Ç‡≤π‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó: ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≤ï ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ, ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤® ‡≤∂‡≥à‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø.

**‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤®‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø**: ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤® ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å. ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ï‡≤® ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á? ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≤É‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤´‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤ï? ‡≤ó‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≥Ä‡≤∞ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤∞? ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤≤ ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø!

#### ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø

‡≤á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó: AI ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤Ö‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü. ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü, ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤ ‡≤®‡≤°‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≥ç‚Äå ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤¨‡≤ü‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

**‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å AI ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤•‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ü‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü**: ‡≤®‡≤ü‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü "‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤π‡≤≥‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≤ø" ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤£ ‡≤§‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤¶‡≥à‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤≠‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤∂ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü. AI ‡≤∏‡≤π ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

#### ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü: ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®

**‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å:**
1. **‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞/‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤ß‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ**: AI ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å?
2. **‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤§‡≤ø**: ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü?
3. **‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤® ‡≤∂‡≥à‡≤≤‡≤ø**: ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Ü?
4. **‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ñ‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤è‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤®Centered
‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å?

```python
# ‚ùå ‡≤Ö‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü
"You are helpful."

# ‚úÖ ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤Ø, ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü
"You are Dr. Sarah Chen, a senior software engineer with 15 years of experience at major tech companies. You explain programming concepts using real-world analogies and always provide practical examples. You're patient with beginners and enthusiastic about helping them understand complex topics."
```

#### ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤§‡≥Ü

‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® AI ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤£:

```python
# ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü 1: ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ï
teacher_prompt = """
You are an experienced programming instructor who has taught thousands of students. 
You break down complex concepts into simple steps, use analogies from everyday life, 
and always check if the student understands before moving on. You're encouraging 
and never make students feel bad for not knowing something.
"""

# ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü 2: ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø
creative_prompt = """
You are a creative writing partner who loves brainstorming wild ideas. You're 
enthusiastic, imaginative, and always build on the user's ideas rather than 
replacing them. You ask thought-provoking questions to spark creativity and 
offer unexpected perspectives that make stories more interesting.
"""

# ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü 3: ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤∞
business_prompt = """
You are a strategic business consultant with an MBA and 20 years of experience 
helping startups scale. You think in frameworks, provide structured advice, 
and always consider both short-term tactics and long-term strategy. You ask 
probing questions to understand the full business context before giving advice.
"""
```

#### ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø:

**‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü**: "‡≤®‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤´‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å?"

```python
# ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ï‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü:

# ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤°‡≥Ä ‡≤®‡≥à‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¨‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≥å‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤ê‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø..."

# ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü:

    "How do I handle user authentication in my web app?", 
    business_prompt

# ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü: "‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤£‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶, ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞
# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤ñ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤§‡≥Ü,
# ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤≠‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≥Ç‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤ñ‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø..."
```

#### ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**1. ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å**: AI ‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≤ø

**matte backend beka yƒÅke:**

**surak·π£ƒÅ**: nim'ma AI API ke·π≠a password hƒÅgide ‚Äì yƒÅdarinda nivege atte frontend JavaScript ge idannu ididdare, nim'ma vebasƒÅi·π≠ina m≈´la kodu opipisuvavaru adannu He·∏∑ida maha·∏çada mƒÅ·∏çi nim'ma AI credits upay≈çgisabahudu. backend ta·πá·πáagege jo·π≠·π≠isalidiruvudu.

**mƒÅtrƒÅ niyantra·πáe mattu nƒ´gara·πáe**: backend nƒ´vu yelli matthu ≈õƒ´ghra ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu mƒÅ·∏çabahudu, upay≈çgakart·πõccinma·π≠·π≠u sahƒ´ti ma·∏çabahudu.

**dƒÅtƒÅ sa·πÉpƒÅdaneya niyamana**: samvƒÅda niva·∏çi irabahudu, apatyakƒÅra sƒÅmagriga·∏∑an Thessƒ´ mƒÅrkavelu, hƒìcchadyanta AI sevega·∏∑annu sa·πÖka·∏∑isuva.

**samaÃÑcƒÅra chu·πõumera·∏çu tantara:**

- **frontend**: upay≈çgakart·πõ muh≈´rtaphurti  
- **backend API**: ƒÅvedaneya pari≈õƒ´lane mattu mƒÅrga·πáe  
- **AI seve**: bƒÅhya ga·πáanƒÅdi mattu uttara racane  
- **paryƒÅvara·πáa mƒÅpaka**: surak·π£ita sƒÅcive mattu suj√±ƒÅ dhƒÅra·πáe

### ƒÅvedane-uttara pravƒÅha artha mƒÅ·∏çiko·∏∑·∏∑uvudu

upay≈çgakart·πõ sande≈õa ko·∏çuvaga yenu na·∏çeyutte anta no·∏çona:  

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User as üë§ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞
    participant Frontend as üåê ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó
    participant API as üîß ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤ê ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç
    participant AI as ü§ñ ‡≤è‡≤ê ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü
    
    User->>Frontend: ‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤™‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤æ "‡≤π‡≤≤‡≥ã ‡≤è‡≤ê!"
    Frontend->>API: POST /hello {"message": "‡≤π‡≤≤‡≥ã ‡≤è‡≤ê!"}
    Note over API: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü<br/>‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
    API->>AI: ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥Ç‡≤™‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
    AI->>API: ‡≤è‡≤ê ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
    Note over API: ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü<br/>‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤¶ ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
    API->>Frontend: {"response": "‡≤π‡≤≤‡≥ã! ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å?"}
    Frontend->>User: ‡≤è‡≤ê ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∂‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
```  
**prati padavannu artha mƒÅ·∏çiko·∏∑·∏∑uva hƒÅge:**  
1. **upay≈çgakart·πõ hƒÅgƒÅ·∏çuvike**: vyakti cƒÅ·π≠ interface nalli type mƒÅ·∏çutta·∏çe  
2. **frontend pari≈õƒ´lane**: JavaScript data na grahisi JSON rƒ´tige r≈´pƒÅnta·πõisuttade  
3. **API pari≈õƒ´lane**: FastAPI kevala Pydantic taraha modelga·∏∑inda ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu pari≈õƒ´lisuttade  
4. **AI sa·πÖkalana**: backend sandarbha (system prompt) ko·π≠·π≠u AI sevegala na kareyuttade  
5. **uttara niva·πõane**: API AI na uttara pa·∏çeduko·∏∑·∏∑i avashyakathe iddare badalƒÅyisuva  
6. **frontend pradar≈õana**: JavaScript adakke uttara cƒÅ·π≠ interface nalli mƒÅ·∏çuttade

### API sa·πÉrachaneya arthakikrÃ•ti

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Frontend
    participant FastAPI
    participant AI Function
    participant GitHub Models
    
    Frontend->>FastAPI: POST /hello {"message": "‡≤®‡≤Æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞ AI!"}
    FastAPI->>AI Function: call_llm(message, system_prompt)
    AI Function->>GitHub Models: API request
    GitHub Models->>AI Function: AI response
    AI Function->>FastAPI: response text
    FastAPI->>Frontend: {"response": "‡≤®‡≤Æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞! ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å?"}
```  
```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å] --> B[‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü]
    B --> C[HTTP POST ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø]
    C --> D[‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥çAPI ‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç]
    D --> E[‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü]
    E --> F[‡≤é‡≤ê ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å]
    F --> G[GitHub ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å API]
    G --> H[‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü]
    H --> I[JSON ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü]
    I --> J[‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£]
    
    subgraph "‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤∞"
        K[CORS ‡≤Æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç]
        L[‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞ ‡≤ö‡≤∞]
        M[‡≤¶‡≥ã‡≤∑ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü]
    end
    
    D --> K
    F --> L
    H --> M
```  
### FastAPI kƒÅryakrama racane mƒÅ·∏çuvudu

nam'ma API na taragatƒì taragatƒì racisona. `api.py` anta hesarina oMdu file na FastAPI ko·∏çige racisi:

```python
# api.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from pydantic import BaseModel
from llm import call_llm
import logging

# ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç API ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≥ï‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
app = FastAPI(
    title="AI Chat API",
    description="A high-performance API for AI-powered chat applications",
    version="1.0.0"
)

# CORS ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø/‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤°‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
class ChatMessage(BaseModel):
    message: str

class ChatResponse(BaseModel):
    response: str

@app.get("/")
async def root():
    """Root endpoint providing API information."""
    return {
        "message": "Welcome to the AI Chat API",
        "docs": "/docs",
        "health": "/health"
    }

@app.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    """Health check endpoint."""
    return {"status": "healthy", "service": "ai-chat-api"}

@app.post("/hello", response_model=ChatResponse)
async def chat_endpoint(chat_message: ChatMessage):
    """Main chat endpoint that processes messages and returns AI responses."""
    try:
        # ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø
        message = chat_message.message.strip()
        if not message:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Message cannot be empty")
        
        logger.info(f"Processing message: {message[:50]}...")
        
        # AI ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø (‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤ü‡≥ç: ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø call_llm ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤®‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å)
        ai_response = await call_llm_async(message, "You are a helpful and friendly assistant.")
        
        logger.info("AI response generated successfully")
        return ChatResponse(response=ai_response)
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error processing chat message: {str(e)}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=5000, reload=True)
```
  
**FastAPI pari·π£kara·πáeya artha mƒÅ·∏çiko·∏∑·∏∑uvudu:**  
- **import** mƒÅ·∏çuttade FastAPI mattu Pydantic na pari≈õƒ´lanege  
- **tƒÅyƒÅrisuttade** svaya·πÅk·πõta API dar≈õanaga·∏∑a (server na·∏çeyuvƒÅga `/docs` nalli)  
- **sampƒÅdisuttade** CORS madhyamavƒÅhini frontend inda vividha laikƒÅ·∏∑adinda ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu anumatisuva  
- **vikalpa** mƒÅ·∏çuttade Pydantic modeli ƒÅvedane/uttara pari≈õƒ´lane mattu dar≈õana savalpa  
- **upay≈çga mƒÅ·∏çuttade** async endpointga·∏∑annu sariyƒÅgi pari≈õƒ´lane mattu uttama kƒÅryak·π£amatege  
- **iruvudu** sarƒ´ya HTTP sthiti ko·∏çuga·∏∑u mattu tappina samƒÅdhƒÅna HTTPException jothege  
- **saha** r≈´paga·∏∑alli logga·∏∑annu koduttade nƒ´gara·πáeya maddi mattu pari≈õƒ´lanege  
- **koduttade** svƒÅsthya pari≈õƒ´lane endpointu, sevƒÅ sthiti he·∏∑uvudu  

**paramparƒÅgata frameworkga·∏∑a mƒìle FastAPI pramukha vi≈õƒì·π£atega·∏∑u:**  
- **svaya·πÅk·πõta pari≈õƒ´lane**: Pydantic modeli dƒÅtƒÅ nirvƒÅhane mƒÅ·π≠·π≠uvaruvudu  
- **antarvartƒ´ya dar≈õana**: `/docs` ge hoga·∏∑uva svaya·πÉk·πõta, pari≈õƒ´litavƒÅda API dar≈õana  
- **type surak·π£ƒÅ**: Python kelavu rƒ´ti sa·πÅketa y≈çjane koda tappuga·∏∑annu niva≈ïtisuva  
- **async sahƒÅya**: anƒìka AI ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu oMde samayadalli niravadhisuva  
- **kƒÅryak·π£amate**: satyavƒÅgi requestga·∏∑a rƒ´ti pari≈õƒ´lane atiyuttama

### CORS annodannu artha mƒÅ·∏çiko·∏∑·∏∑uvudu: web surak·π£ƒÅ carita

CORS (Cross-Origin Resource Sharing) oMdu surak·π£aka digavƒÅhna hƒÅgide, yƒÅrendare binna ma·π≠·π≠alƒÅ·∏çu mƒÅ·∏çalu anumati ko·∏çuvudƒÅgi n≈ç·∏çuttade. idu yƒÅke mukhya mattu nim'ma anukrama·πáikeyalli yenu pƒÅthrapƒÅ·∏çuttade anta tiliduko·∏∑·∏∑ona.

#### CORS yenu mattu idu yƒÅke irutƒì?

**sa·πÅ≈õaya**: yƒÅvudƒÅdaru vebasƒÅi·π≠u nim'ma hesarinda nim'ma bƒìlige ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu mƒÅ·∏çabahuda endare? adu surak·π£ƒÅ ma·∏çuvala! ba·∏çigega·∏∑u "same-origin policy" m≈´lake ƒ´dannu avarjemge niveyuttade.

**same-origin policy**: ba·∏çige nƒ´vu pagege tindi ƒÅ·∏çida domain, port mattu protocol nalli mƒÅtra ƒÅvedanega·∏∑annu m≈ç·∏çvatte.

**vƒÅstavika udƒÅhara·πáa**: oMdu apartment bhavana surak·π£aka ‚Äì kevala nivƒÅsiga·∏∑u (same origin) bhavana ko·∏çalƒÅgide. nƒ´vu obba mitra (binnƒÅ origin) baredi·∏ça kareyalu surak·π£akanu to·∏∑aguvudu.

#### nim'ma abhivrÃ•ddhi parisaradalli CORS

abhivrÃ•ddhi shƒì·π£a nim'ma frontend mattu backend vividha ports nalli na·∏çeyuttade:  
- frontend: `http://localhost:3000` (athavƒÅ HTML sƒ´dhƒÅgi teredaga `file://`)  
- backend: `http://localhost:5000`  

iduvu oMde ka·πá·πáuhƒÅ·πá·∏ça nƒ´·∏çuvudilla yƒÅva·∏çe avantara!

```python
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

app = FastAPI(__name__)
CORS(app)   # ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü: "‡≤á‡≤§‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥å‡≤≤‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤à API ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤"
```
  
**CORS paricaya yeda prakara:**  
- **ADD mƒÅ·∏çuttade** vishƒì·π£a HTTP headers jothege API uttaraga·∏∑ige, idu ba·∏çigege "ƒ´ binna origin ƒÅvedane anumatide" antu he·∏∑idda  
- **pƒÅlgottade** "prƒÅra·πÉbhika" ƒÅvedanega·∏∑u (ba·∏çigega·∏∑u modala kƒÅrya ke·∏∑abekƒÅdare nivu parƒ´k·π£eya mƒÅ·∏çuttade)  
- **nivƒÅrisuttade** "CORS nƒ´ti dvara ba·∏çiga nivƒÅda" anta brauzar console dalli tappu

#### CORS surak·π£ƒÅ: abhivrÃ•ddhi vs utpƒÅdan

```python
# üö® ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø: ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü (‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤Ü‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤)
CORS(app)

# ‚úÖ ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤°‡≥ä‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
CORS(app, origins=["https://yourdomain.com", "https://www.yourdomain.com"])

# üîí ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
if app.debug:  # ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç
    CORS(app, origins=["http://localhost:3000", "http://127.0.0.1:3000"])
else:  # ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç
    CORS(app, origins=["https://yourdomain.com"])
```
  
**idu yƒÅke mukhya**: abhivrÃ•ddhi nalli `CORS(app)` nim'ma m≈´ka·∏∑uvina hatadi·π≠·π≠u ‚Äì sulabhavƒÅgi kottade, ƒÅdare surak·π£ita alla. utpƒÅdanadalli tappadanta websitega·∏∑u nim'ma API nalli ·∏çƒÅka ko·∏çuttade endu niyamisabekƒÅguttade.

#### sƒÅmƒÅnya CORS paristhitigalu mattu pari·π£kƒÅraga·∏∑u

| paristhiti           | samasya                 | pari·π£kƒÅra                            |  
|---------------------|-------------------------|------------------------------------|  
| **sthala abhivrÃ•ddhi**    | frontend backendge sigalilla | FastAPI ge CORSMiddleware seerisuvudu  |  
| **GitHub Pages + Heroku** | utpƒÅdita frontend APIge sigalilla | nim'ma GitHub Pages URL na CORS dvara seerisu  |  
| **vi≈õi·π£·π≠a ·∏çomƒìn**        | utpƒÅdanadalli CORS tappuga·∏∑u | CORS dvara nim'ma domainge anur≈´pa mƒÅ·∏çi  |  
| **mo·∏çi apilike≈õan**      | apile Web API sigalilla  | nim'ma app-ina domain athavƒÅ `*`niyama savala·πÖkita r≈´padi·πÅda upay≈çga  

**uttama s≈´tra**: nim'ma brauzar developer tools nalli Network tab n≈´·∏çi CORS headerga·∏∑annu no·∏çabahudu. erada uttarada Access-Control-Allow-Origin jothege header e·π£·π≠u iddƒìnte no·∏çi.

### tappuga·∏∑annu niyantara·πáe mattu pari≈õƒ´lane

nim'ma API elli sarƒ´ya tappu niyama mƒÅ·∏çida no·∏çi:

```python
# ‡≤®‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
if not message:
    return jsonify({"error": "Message field is required"}), 400
```
  
**pramukha pari≈õƒ´lane sid'dhƒÅnta:**  
- ƒÅvedana m≈´lagƒÅgi ƒÅvashyaka mƒÅ·π≠uga·∏∑annu pari≈õƒ´lade  
- artha pur·πáavƒÅda tappina sande≈õaga·∏∑u JSON rƒ´tige ko·∏çuttade  
- sƒÅrthaka HTTP sthiti codega·∏∑u hƒÅkuva (400 tappu ƒÅvedanega·∏∑ige)  
- frontend abhivrÃ•ddhaka·∏∑ige spash·π≠a pari≈õ≈çdhane sahƒÅya ko·∏çuvudu

## nim'ma backend na set up mƒÅ·∏çuvudu mattu na·∏çeyuvudu

ƒ´ga nƒÅvu AI sa·πÖkalana mattu FastAPI server tayƒÅr mƒÅ·∏çiddƒÅre, ellƒÅvan·∏∑·∏∑i na·∏çeyalu beku. setup prakriye Python avashyakaga·∏∑annu iruvisuvudu, parisaravagi bƒì·∏çikega·∏∑annu she·π≠·π≠u mƒÅ·∏çuvudu, mattu abhivrÃ•ddhi server na pampi·π≠·π≠u.

### Python parisarada sƒÅdhane

nim'ma Python abhivrÃ•ddhi parisara na set up mƒÅ·∏çona. Virtual environments hƒÅge bƒÅvariyuta ide ‚Äì yƒÅva projejk·π≠u adhika sthƒÅna paricƒÅlana mƒÅduttade (cada one hosa sƒÅmagriga·∏∑u mattu avashyakaga·∏∑u jothege, paraspara sƒÅhasasamarthakathe illa).

```bash

# ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø (‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö ‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤†‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü)

# ‡≤Ö‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø (‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏/‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç)
source ./venv/bin/activate

# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø, ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø:
# venv\Scripts\activate

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

```
  
**nƒÅvu hege mƒÅ·∏çiddƒìve:**  
- oMdu nim'ma m≈ç·π≠·π≠u Python hƒÅkuge, yƒÅvudakke bere yƒÅvude a≈õraya mƒÅ·∏çuvudilla  
- activate mƒÅdide he·∏∑uvudu terminal alli idu kƒÅrya mƒÅdutte anta  
- avashyakaga·∏∑u install mƒÅ·∏çide: OpenAI AI a·π£·π≠ira≈õakti ge, FastAPI web API ge, Uvicorn a·πÖga server ge mattu python-dotenv gupta mƒÅ·∏çalu

**pramukha ƒÅva≈õyakaga·∏∑u vivaravƒÅgi**:  
- **FastAPI**: ƒÅdhunika, vegavanta Web framework svaya·πÅk·πõta API dar≈õana sahita  
- **Uvicorn**: vegavƒÅgi FastAPI anukrama·πáika na·∏çeyuva ASGI server  
- **OpenAI**: GitHub Models mattu OpenAI API jothege adhikƒÅrika pustaka  
- **python-dotenv**: .env file galinda surak·π£ita parisaravagi parivartisuva

### parisaravagi samay≈çjana: guptaga·∏∑annu surak·π£ita mƒÅ·∏çuvudu

API na prƒÅrambhamƒÅ·∏çuva munna·π≠a, ondhu atiyavashyaka web abhivrÃ•ddhi pa·π≠a·πáike - nim'ma guptaga·∏∑annu yƒÅke surak·π£ita mƒÅ·∏çabƒìku anta. parisaravagi samay≈çjana hƒÅge oMdu rak·π£ita vƒÅ≈õi vike≈õa ‚Äì kevala nim'ma app ge use maduva hakku ide.

#### parisaravagi samay≈çjana yenu?

**parisaravagi samay≈çjana na`nn guptƒÅka·∏∑a dhanƒÅvar·πái·∏çi ghƒÅ·π≠aka** ‚Äì nƒ´vu he·∏∑uva m≈´lya vastu·∏∑annu adaralli horuvarisuvudu matte nim'ma (matte nim'ma app) mƒÅtra tannadu ko·∏∑·∏∑uttade. sƒ´dhƒÅgirisi guptavƒÅgada mƒÅ·∏çuvaru kode inside idde (ellavƒÅrig≈´ no·∏çabahudu) avaru kuri no·∏çuva mani·π£·π≠ada bhƒÅga.

**iduvudake paryƒÅyatmaka:**  
- **tappu mƒÅrga**: nim'ma password sticky note alli baredu monitor mele hƒÅkida he·∏∑uvudu  
- **sariyƒÅgi mƒÅrga**: password nim'ma surak·π£ita password menƒìjara·∏∑·∏∑i iruvudu

#### parisaravagi samay≈çjaneya mukhyate

```python
# üö® ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ç ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤°‡≤ø - API ‡≤ï‡≥Ä ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤á‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
client = OpenAI(
    api_key="ghp_1234567890abcdef...",  # ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ç ‡≤ï‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å!
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference"
)

# ‚úÖ ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø - API ‡≤ï‡≥Ä ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å
client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ["GITHUB_TOKEN"],  # ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference"
)
```
  
**nim'ma guptaga·∏∑u hardcode mƒÅ·∏çuva samayadalli:**  
1. **version control prƒÅka·π≠ya**: nim'ma git repository yƒÅrigƒì access ide avaru nim'ma API key n≈ç·∏çabahudu  
2. **sarvajana repository**: GitHub ge push mƒÅ·∏çiddare key samp≈´r·πáavƒÅgi praka·π≠a  
3. **team hƒì·∏∑uva**: bere developerga·∏∑u nim'ma API key upay≈çgisuva  
4. **surak·π£ƒÅ bhanga**: yƒÅradaru nim'ma API key kaVcukoNDare adannu upay≈çgisuva AI creditgala ha·πá·∏çƒÅdare

#### nim'ma environment file na set mƒÅ·∏çuvudu

backend directory nalli `.env` file tayƒÅr mƒÅ·∏çi. ivasthu nim'ma guptaga·∏∑u stha·∏∑ƒ´ya rak·π£a·πáeyalli iruvudakke:

```bash
# .env ‡≤´‡≥à‡≤≤‡≥ç - ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å Git ‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ç ‡≤ï‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≥Å

```
  
**.env file artha mƒÅ·∏çiko·∏∑·∏∑uvudu:**  
- **oMdu rahasya pratyƒìka kƒìlinalilx** `KEY=value` mƒÅrga·∏çalli  
- **samak·π£epiNAre** illa `=` cho·π≠·π≠alalli  
- **koti cita** illa m≈´lyaga·∏∑a ƒÅsapƒÅsa (ƒÅmuma·π≠e)  
- **·π≠ippa·πáiga·∏∑u** `#` inda ƒÅrambhamƒÅ·∏çuva

#### nim'ma GitHub vyakti gatƒÅvaiyƒÅyu·π≠a token tayƒÅrisuvudu

nim'ma GitHub token nim'ma app ge GitHub AI sevaga·∏∑annu upay≈çgisuva adhikƒÅra ni·∏çuva hƒìgagƒÅgiruttade:

**tera mƒÅrga kramayƒÅva·∏∑i:**  
1. **GitHub Set·π≠ingsge ho·∏çi** ‚Üí Developer settings ‚Üí Personal access tokens ‚Üí Tokens (classic)  
2. **"Generate new token (classic)" nalilc lƒÅbhyamƒÅ·∏çi state**  
3. **samƒÅpti samaaya ni·∏çu** (30 dino parƒ´k·π£a·πáege, hecchu kƒÅlaga·∏∑akke sthƒÅyi)  
4. **adhikƒÅraga·∏∑annu tƒ´·∏∑iyiri**: "repo" mattu bere sƒÅdhyateya nir≈´pa·πáa mƒìle tikki  
5. **token tayƒÅrisu** mattu turuntu copy mƒÅ·∏çi (mati no·∏çalu sƒÅdhyavilla!)  
6. **.env file ge o·∏∑age olidisiri**

```bash
# ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¨ ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü (‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø!)
GITHUB_TOKEN=ghp_1A2B3C4D5E6F7G8H9I0J1K2L3M4N5O6P7Q8R
```
  
#### Python nalli parisaravagi samay≈çjanaga·∏∑annu hƒÅkuvudu

```python

from dotenv import load_dotenv

# .env ‡≤´‡≥à‡≤≤‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞ ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø

# ‡≤à‡≤ó ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
api_key = os.environ.get("GITHUB_TOKEN")

    raise ValueError("GITHUB_TOKEN not found in environment variables!")

    api_key=api_key,
    base_url="https://models.github.ai/inference"
)
```
  
**ƒ´ ko·∏çu yenu mƒÅ·∏çuttade:**  
- nim'ma .env file na load mƒÅ·∏çi parisaravagi samay≈çjanaga·∏∑annu Python ge anuk≈´·∏∑a mƒÅ·∏çuttade  
- ƒÅvedavalada API key iddƒìnte anta pari≈õƒ´lane mƒÅ·∏çuttade (sarala tappina nirƒ´k·π£e)  
- token illa iddare he·∏∑uva tappu baruttade  
- token na surak·π£ita vagadƒÅda upay≈çga mƒÅ·∏çuttade, ko·∏çina bƒÅga·πÅdu pariga·πáisuva illa

#### Git surak·π£ƒÅ: `.gitignore` file

nim'ma `.gitignore` file Git ge yaava filega·∏∑annu anusarisuva illa endu he·∏∑uttade:

**ƒ´dara mukhyate**: `.env` ge `.gitignore` seerisi, Git nƒ´vu niyamita kramadalli nim'ma guptaga·∏∑annu GitHub ge accidental hƒÅkuvudakkiro na·∏çeyuvudilla.

#### vividha parisaraga·∏∑u, vividha guptaga·∏∑u

v·πõddhƒÅnta padavƒ´ya appga·∏∑u vividha parisaraga·∏∑ige vividha API keys na upay≈çgisuttave:
